國科會補助專題研究計畫成果報告自評表 
請就研究內容與原計畫相符程度、達成預期目標情況、研究成果之學
術或應用價值（簡要敘述成果所代表之意義、價值、影響或進一步發
展之可能性）、是否適合在學術期刊發表或申請專利、主要發現或其他
有關價值等，作一綜合評估。 
4. 請就研究內容與原計畫相符程度、達成預期目標情況作一綜合評估 
█ 達成目標 
說明： 
預期成果： 
傳統空調系統中以冰水主機之耗電量最大，因此大部分電能需量卸載系統均以
卸載冰水主機為主，但在卸載冰水主機用電的同時，將造成冰水溫度上升，導
致現場空調箱及小型送風機的冷卻能力降低，進而使得室內溫度上升，影響整
棟大樓的空調環境熱舒適度。有鑑於此本計畫將研究在空調供應的室內環境空
間中，運用建築能源管理系統定義有效溫度(Effective Temperature ,ET*)區間，
在不影響空調環境熱舒適度指標值(Predicted Mean Vote ,PMV)之前提下，配合
需量反應機制對空調系統設備進行需量卸載最佳化控制。 
   實際成果： 
計畫中透過裝設在實驗現場的 8 組室內溫濕度偵測器，長時間記錄 8 組實驗
環境區域內室內乾球溫度及相對濕度的變化量，並將 ISO 7730 PMV 計算程式
運用於可程式控制器(Program Logic Controller, PLC)內作 PMV 值連續計算，
其結果回饋給現場空調設備作為控制條件之依據，成功地執行需量卸載並將
現場環境溫濕度控制在預期的 PMV 值(0~0.5)。 
   差    異： 
   實際成果與預期成果無差異。 
 
  
  
子計畫五：多重智慧型代理人在智慧電網中自動協調與自我痊
癒之研究 
共同主持人：清華大學資訊工程學系  蘇豐文教授 
 
摘要 
因現有電力公司的通信系統採用封閉式建置，
因此配電系統之調度仍然以集中的方式進行，所
有的即時資訊均需要傳送到區域調度中心進行
研判與決策。故無論是故障的分析、排除與復電，
或是與各分散式電源的溝通與控制，都必須透過
區域調度中心進行資訊交換。當智慧型電網建置
完成後，由於網路資訊系統的建置，分散式系統
可以輔助現有的集中式系統，提高供電的可靠度。
本計畫建構在智慧型的分散式系統上並採用多
代理人系統的自我協調溝通方式解決現有電力
系統中的故障回復問題，減少因故障發生導致的
經濟活動上的損失；並導入市場協商機制，降低
尖峰負載量及發電成本等，以增進未來智慧型電
網的運轉效益。 
關鍵詞：分散式演算法、多代理人系統、市場協
商機制、電力回復 
1. 前言 
分散式多代理人系統為一軟體系統。該系統
由許多智慧型軟體代理人程式組成。每一個代理
人程式可以負責一部分的計算、控制或協商的機
制，藉由競爭與合作以及相互間溝通與協調，達
到整體及局部最佳化表現的目的；與傳統的集中
式控制方式有所不同的部分，在於當某些代理人
因軟體、硬體或通訊系統發生故障時，並不會影
響整體的運作。單一代理人的失效，僅影響到部
分決策可用的資訊，其他代理人所提供的資訊仍
然可以做為決策之用。 
智慧型電網代理人系統的性能指標有：1)電
價價格及 2)停電回復時間。這些性能指標取決於
代理人系統內建的決策支援系統、機器學習系統
與代理人對話與協商系統。代理人溝通合作系統
則可透過 FIPA(Foundation for Intelligent 
Physical Agents) 所 制 定 的 ACL (Agent 
Communication Language)並搭配遊戲對局理論
中的多代理人協商機制進行之。分散式代理人決
策系統可藉由經濟學上市場競爭原理取得系統
最佳化表現之目的。電力系統的市場機制則可藉
由分散式多代理人的制作與模擬來了解最佳化
電力輸配的問題解決方法。 
2. 研究目的 
隨著科技的進步，工商業的興盛，電力系統
無法正常運作對社會所造成的損害與日俱增，復
電問題也逐漸受到重視，此外，傳統所使用的電
力批發市場逐漸的被零售的電力市場架構所取
代，在許多國家當中，各項針對市場設計的問題
正激烈被討論中，比如如何避免市場壟斷，如何
正確實做出電力零售市場並增加市場整體的利
潤，以及如何在最短的時間內以最低成本恢復斷
電區域的電力系統，皆成為近年來相當重要的討
論議題。 
如何能在意外發生之後，盡可能的恢復停電
區域的電力，稱之為復電問題。在本計畫中，我
們將傳統的電力輸配系統視為一個智慧型電網，
在智慧電網中的每一個元件亦皆可視為一個智
慧代理人(例如：發電機、開關、電力區域)。透
過這些代理人之間的溝通協調機制，為電力系統
中的復電問題提供最佳解決方案，並透過電力市
場的供需協調機制，能夠達到供應者與需求者之
間最大利益的平衡，可以達到電力市場的拓樸的
重新分配，降低電力的輸出成本，提高發電效

子計畫五：多重智慧型代理人在智慧電網中自動協調與自我痊
癒之研究 
共同主持人：台北科技大學自動化所  蔡孟伸教授 
 
摘要 
 
傳統的配電系統(Distribution System)係
由許多的饋線(Feeder)所相互連接而成的一個
網路。饋線與饋線之間通常安裝數個連絡開
關(Tie Switch)；饋線上也會配置數個區段開
關(Sectionalizing Switch)。當配電系統發生故
障時，調度員可以藉由改變開關之開、關狀
態達到故障的隔離與完成負載區域復電等目
標。在本研究計畫中，利用多代理人系統
(Multi-Agent System, MAS)的分散式特性及
可以互相交換訊息的機制，當配電系統發生
意外事故時，代理人系統可以執行智慧型配
電自動化復電規劃。系統中的每個代理人都
可自動和獨立的運作，且可以視需要去執行
有關的復電規劃。藉由配電系統的相關訊息
的溝通，代理人可以平行快速地進行復電工
作，進而得以降低復電過程所需的等待時間。
本研究計畫將於代理人開發環境 JADE 平台
(Java Agent DEvelopment Framework)上，運用
BDI(Belief, Desire, and Intention)智慧型多代
理人系統並結合經驗式(heuristic)規則復電決
策，對配電系統因故障事故而造成停電的負
載區域執行電力的回復程序。透過復電規劃，
配電系統將具有自癒(self-healing)的能力。最
後，本研究計畫期望除了能夠達到最大的復
電區域外，也由於多代理人系統的分散式特
性及可相互交換傳遞訊息的機制，每一個代
理人都可以進行復電規劃，進而使得復電過
程的所需等待時間得以被減少。 
關鍵詞：配電系統、復電決策、BDI 智慧型
代理人。 
 
Abstract 
By changing the status of switches on 
distribution feeders, service to de-energized 
customers can be restored after an occurrence of 
a fault. In this project, software intelligent 
agents are installed inside each switch and 
feeder. These agents form a distributed 
multi-agent environment. By utilizing the 
characteristics of information sharing, 
multi-agent systems (MAS) can be applied for 
the power distribution system service 
restoration task. Each software agent is running 
autonomously and is able to exchange 
information within limited distance. By 
exchanging the information among agents, 
service restoration can be performed in parallel. 
As a result, the outage period can be reduced. 
BDI (Believe-Desire-Intention) agents are 
implemented in this project for group and zone 
service restoration for power distribution 
systems. Binary search tree is used in each 
agent in order to identify adequate switching 
actions during the service restoration planning 
stage. The proposed MAS is implemented on 
JADE (Java Agent DEvelopment) platform.  
The simulation results show that the proposed 
BDI (Believe-Desire-Intention) based service 
restoration agent system is capable of providing 
adequate restoration switching plan in several 
scenarios. 
 
Keywords: Distribution Systems, Service 
restoration, BDI Agent. 
 
1. Introduction 
A typical distribution system is formed by 
interconnection many loads through conductors.  
These loads are partitioned by many switches.  
The switches can be divided into two types: 
normally closed sectionalized switches and 
normally opened tie switches.  The status of 
  
outage zone/switch relation table is built by 
leader agents. The leader agents will identify an 
adequate restoration switching plan based on 
this table. The switching action decision is send 
to the relevant switch agents to restore service 
to customers. In order to verify and validate the 
proposed MAS system, a distribution system is 
used.  The results show that the proposed MAS 
is able to propose adequate service restoration 
plan with fewer communication cost compared 
with centralized approach. 
2. Problem Formulation of 
Distribution System Service 
Restoration 
When a fault occurred in a distribution 
system, service to customers may be interrupted.  
The switches adjacent to the faulted area are 
opened to isolate the fault first.  Service 
restoration task is performed in order to restore 
service to the outage area as much as possible 
within the shortest period of time by changing 
the status of switches within the outage area.  
The service restoration problem can be 
formulated as following: 
1
n
i i
i
Min x load
=
⋅∑  
1, if the i-th zone is de-energized
0, if the i-th zone is energized     i
x = 

 
where n is the total number of zones. Loadi 
is the load current within the i-th zone. 
The constraints of the service restoration 
problem considered in this project include: 1) 
the line current of all conductors must be within 
the conductor capacity; 2) the total served loads 
of each feeder must be within its capacity; 3) 
the radial topology must be maintained; 4) the 
voltage profile of each feeder should be 
maintained within allowable range.  The 
distribution system to be considered in this 
project has following characteristics: 
(1) Only the primary distribution feeder 
(11.4/22.8 kV) is considered. 
(2) Three-phase laterals with switches that 
are connected to adjacent feeders are 
considered. 
(3) Three phase currents and voltages are 
considered simultaneously. 
(4) The voltage drop is not considered. 
Traditional service restoration approaches 
considered the service restoration problem as a 
constrained optimization problem [1-5].  Thus, 
the information of whole system is needed 
during the problem solving process.  This 
requires a powerful computer with a large 
amount of memory to handle a large scale of 
distribution system.  On the other hand, the 
MAS approach does not require a powerful 
computer system since the computation loads 
are distributed into many smaller 
computers/controllers. Also, the MAS approach 
only considers the information within outage 
area; while the centralized approach requires all 
information of the system. 
3. BDI Agents Approach for Service 
Restoration Problems 
In recent artificial intelligent related 
researches, intelligent agents have gotten a lot 
of attention because of their autonomous 
behavior. These agents can act by themselves 
due to the environmental changes. When these 
agents are not able to accomplish the 
pre-designed task, they may exchange 
information among agents in order to solve the 
problem cooperatively.  Several agent 
architectures were proposed in the past, the 
deliberative architecture, reactive architecture, 
learning based architecture and layered 
architecture.  Some of these architectures were 
applied for service restoration problems. 
A layered architecture required a 
centralized agent that handles all the necessary 
communication and information between lower 
layer agents.  Deliberative MAS architecture is 
proposed in [7].  However, the decision 
making within the agents is based on the 
heuristics.  Thus, the system may not be able 
to find a solution. In [8], a BDI 
(Believe-Desire-Intension) based MAS system 
is proposed which utilized a simple decision 
tree to identify the restoration plan.  In this 
project, a enhanced BDI model is developed by 
using zone/switch relational model for decision 
making process. The zone-switch relational 
model is constructed by an agent that is 
responsible for service restoration. 
The typical concept of BDI-Based agents is 
shown in Fig. 1. The internal status of 
  
Detailed description of agent based 
restoration procedure is discussed as following 
stages: 
Stage 1) Identify the Service Restoration 
Leader Agent 
After the occurrence of a fault, the status of 
the switches next to the faulted section is 
marked as “LOCKED_OPEN”.  The changing 
of the switch status is the stimulation to the 
MAS. The agents next to the faulted section ask 
the status of their source and load side agents. 
The agent located at the load side of the faulted 
section is identified as the leader agent. If the 
fault is located on a simple line section, then 
only one load side agent exists and it is assigned 
as the leader agent.  On the other hand, if the 
fault is located on a line section with several 
branches, all load side switch agents will be 
assigned as the leader agents. 
After the leader agents are identified, each 
leader agent will start building the topology of 
outage areas by querying the load side agents 
and all adjacent feeders. Based on the 
information, a zone/switch relation model that 
represents the legal combination of outage 
zones is built by each leader agent. The leader 
agents are responsible for the restoration service 
to its load side area. 
Stage 2) Identify the outage area 
The leader agent searches the outage area 
by querying the load side switch agents. If the 
status of the switch of the queried agent is 
closed, the switch information is passed to the 
leader agent and the query is passed further to 
the load side. On the other hand, if the status of 
the queried switch is open, the switch agent 
passes the information to the leader agent. After 
all tie switches response to the leader agent, the 
outage area can be identified. 
Stage 3) Identify the available ampacity of all 
adjacent feeders 
In this step, the tie switch agents is tried to 
identify the adjacent feeder available ampacity. 
Since agents can only communicate their 
adjacent neighbors, this step is similar to step 2. 
Stage 4) Leader agent searches for service 
restoration plan 
After the available ampacity of all adjacent 
feeders are obtained, the leader agent checks if 
any feeder is able to pick-up all loads within the 
outage area. If the outage area can be picked up 
by single switch operation, leader agent will ask 
the associated tie switch agent to close the 
switch.  If none of the feeder has enough 
ampacity to pick-up all loads within the outage 
area, zone restoration is performed. For zone 
restoration, a three-step procedure is described 
as following. 
Step1: Build the zone/switch relation table. 
The leader agent builds the zone/switch 
relation table based on queried information. In 
order to build the zone/switch relation table, 
possible outage zone combinations needs to be 
identified first. The outage zone combinations 
can be expressed as Eq. (1): 
1

or more switches; and at least one of these 
switches is a tie-switch. Note that the total 
number of combinations of N outage zones can 
be expressed as Eq. (2).

The number of elements in S is far less than 
the number obtain in (2) due to the topological 
constraints. After the elements in S are 
identified, the outage zone/switch relation table 
can be built. 
Step 2: Search restorable zones. 
The leader agent searches for possible 
restoration zones based on the outage 
zone/switch relation table and the available 
ampacity of adjacent feeders. The available 
ampacities of adjacent feeders are compared 
with the loads in the outage zone/switch relation 
table in decent order. A possible zone transfer 
solution can be identified after the comparisons. 
The restoration search is terminated if none of 
adjacent feeder is able to pick up any load in the 
outage zone.  Note that it is possible that more 
than one feeder may be identified in this step. 
Step 3: Identify the switch actions. 
Based on the feeder(s) identified in Step2, 
the tie switch(es) between the feeder(s) and the 
selected outage zones is(are) identified. If more

restoration. The simulation result shows that the 
proposed MAS system can provide adequate 
switch plan the same as centralized based 
service restoration system used in present 
control center with fewer message passing cost.

 主要成果

Framework)上，運用 BDI(Belief, Desire, and Intention)智慧型多代理人系統並結合經
驗式(heuristic)規則復電決策，對配電系統因故障事故而造成停電的負載區域執行電
力的回復程序。透過復電規劃，配電系統將具有自癒(self-healing)的能力。 
 本研究計畫期望除了能夠達到最大的復電區域外，也由於多代理人系統的分散式特
性及可相互交換傳遞訊息的機制，每一個代理人都可以進行復電規劃，進而使得復
電過程的所需等待時間得以被減少。 
 價值與影響



及證書外，有三場演講：第一場是由美國 Intel公司的 Mark Bohr 講演 The Evolution 
of Scaling from the Homogeneous Era to the Heterogeneous Era，第二場是由
日本豐田汽車的 Takumi Matsumoto講演 Approach Toward Achieving Sustainable 
Mobility，第三場是由法國 CEA的 Bernard Dieny 講演 Extended Scalability and 
Functionalities of MRAM Based on Thermally Assisted Writing。下午 1:30-5:00
聆聽在 Session 5: Memory Technology – PCM and RRAM 發表的七篇論文。 
 
晚上是大會的 reception。遇到很多舊識相談甚歡且談到一些研究合作的可能性。

Semiconductor for Power Devices?。

五、建議 
iedm是電子元件領域最重要的國際研討會，也是 IEEE Electron Device 學會的年會。
在這會議中，來自全球頂尖的實驗室（大學及研究機構）展示他們一年來電子元件最
新的研究成果。參加這個會議可以瞭解目前電子元件的發展趨勢，也可以和來自世界
各地的電子元件專家相互切磋。我們應多多鼓勵校內同仁參與此會議以提升學校在電
子元件的研究能量。 
附件：所發表的論文 
 
bipolar HfOX device. With a wide margin of ~20 between the 
HRS and LRS, the potential for more than 1010 cycles is 
demonstrated. To prevent the HRS from damages by high 
compliance current [11], the SET current compliance is 
about 100 μA for the device without HRS degradation 
during endurance test. In Fig. 12, the retention results at 150 
and 220 °C for 10 hrs prove strong immunity to the thermal 
disturbance for both the HRS and LRS. The lifetime of 
resistance states at 220 °C are expected to exceed 10 yrs. 
The reliabilities of read and program/erase disturb are also 
explored. As shown in Fig. 13, inserting a AlOX layer 
between HfOX and bottom electrode elevates the 
time-to-disturb voltage up to 0.5 V, providing an extra 0.1 V 
margin for read disturb. The AlOx layer doesn’t affect the 
resistive switching characteristics of the HfOX device [5]. 
There are no program/erase disturbance issues for the 
resistive device with driving transistor (1T1R device) when 
the large parasitic capacitance between the transistor and 
resistive device is eliminated [5]. The lack of a current path 
between the transistor and the resistive device prevents 
parasitic capacitance discharge. A 1 kb array with HfOX cells 
has been successfully fabricated and shows 100 % device 
yield after forming. The insert of Fig. 14 shows the 
distributions of HRS and LRS for the 1 kb array after 1, 10k, 
and 1M cycles by 40 ns pulse. Compared to the initial 
distribution, the distributions of HRS and LRS become more 
and more fluctuant with increasing cycling number. The 
method of ramping up VRESET can be used to verify the HRS; 
however, this simple approach of ramping up operation 
voltage does not always work for the verification of LRS 
because a portion of the LRS region may increase in 
resistance, effectively leading to a unipolar RESET [5]. A 
novel verification method of higher VSET to the device after 
performing RESET step (HVAR) is proposed to suppress 
soft errors of LRS and improve the LRS distribution [5]. As 
shown in Fig. 14, by effective verification, the HRS and LRS 
of the cells in the 1 kb array are more than 100 kΩ and less 
than 10 kΩ, respectively. Table I summarizes the 
characteristics of bipolar RRAM devices including TaOX, 
Al2O3, and HfOX. The HfOX bipolar device without noble 
metals is one of the promising candidates owing to sub-ns 
switching speed, low power, high device yield, and robust 
reliabilities.  
Unipolar switching in the HfOX system is also studied 
with Ni electrodes. By verification, the endurance exceeds 
more than 104 times without any soft errors during cycling, 
as shown in Fig. 15.  
 
Future Challenges 
 
There are still challenges for bipolar RRAM before 
commercialization. The resistive switching of the device at 
low current of μA level is required for low power application. 
Low current operation below 1 μA has been demonstrated in 
RRAM devices with AlOXNY and WOX films [8,13]. As the 
operation current is reduced to below 100 μA, increasing 
soft-errors of LRS for the device during cycling are observed, 
because the LRS is higher and begins to overlap with the 
HRS. The HfOX bipolar device exhibits a good endurance of 
104 cycles at 30 μA, as shown in Fig. 16. The HRS/LRS 
ratio is more than 50 and there are no soft errors in any cycle. 
Smaller transistors offer less current but do not take up 
proportionately less voltage. Therefore, the second challenge 
for the bipolar device is developing a cross-point array 
structure for high density application. Figure 17 shows the 
schematic diagram of I-V curve for the bipolar device with 
bi-directional diode. The non-Ohmic LRS is expected to 
avoid the sneak path in cross-point array. In addition to 
bi-directional diode [14], other bi-directional selectors 
(ovonic threshold switches [15] and mixed ionic electronic 
conductors [16]) or RRAM structures (self-rectifying RRAM 
[17] and complementary resistive switch [18]) are also under 
development.  
Unipolar RRAM also faces challenges. Low switching 
speed, unstable operation, and high power are found in the 
unipolar RRAM. These critical issues need to be solved to 
improve the switching characteristics and reliability of the 
unipolar RRAM. 
 
Conclusion 
 
The progresses and characteristics of some metal oxides 
in the RRAM field are reviewed. HfOX bipolar RRAM has 
advantages of not requiring noble metals, sub-ns speed, 
excellent reliabilities, and good uniformity of resistance 
states in the array level. A device endurance of 104 cycles at 
30 μA indicates the promising potential for low current 
application. Suitable bi-directional selectors or RRAM 
structures need to be developed to implement the cross-point 
array for high density NVM application.

masses along normal direction. Although the effective gate-insulator thickness can be reduced by the 
strained-Si engineering to have a larger effective mass in normal direction, the contributions of the 
effective-mass strained-Si engineering to the current enhancements are considerably small for the high-k 
MOSFETs. The on-current of high-k gate-insulator MOSFETs is limited by quantum-mechanical 
inversion layer whether the strained-Si techniques are applied or not.
